# Prompt Log

- [Full Augment Code Log](./pure-augment-log.md)
  - Opus 4.7 as the Agent Coordinator (4.8 is more expensive, and I am running out of budget =P) 
  - This isn't really readable, but I'll include it for the sake of transparency.
- [Augment Code Specification File](./augment-spec.md)

## Augment Code - Log Abbreviation

```text
I have been offered a job interview for a position which has provided me with this initial task in the form of a PDF document titled 'AEM_Content_Discovery_Agent_Brief.pdf'. Please read through it, understand what it wants me to build, and then come back with a first draft, which we can use to transition into an ideation session.
```

```text
We also need a multi-step approach that includes the following steps: first, an incoming prompt, then sending it to LLM to improve the prompt, followed by RAG and then returning the result.
```

```text
Node.js (Node 22) + Gemma 4.26b for an embedding model — not sure yet. We need to keep planning. For now, I'm just adding some notes here.
```

```text
We also need a 'seeding' script that utilises the AEM API or MCP to create content fragments. We also need to use Faker.js to create 'realistic' content. We need 'n' fragments for each locale. See https://experienceleague.adobe.com/en/docs/experience-manager-cloud-service/content/ai-in-aem/local-development-with-ai-tools#aem-quickstart-mcp-server for more information.
```

```text
[...]
Some back-and-forth about what the Ollama model IDs are, what the content-fragment structure should look like, the target locales, and the quantity of items we want to seed, as well as similar preparatory work.
[...]
```

```text
[...]
There was some discussion about the source of the live content in AEM versus the local, static content stored as data.json. SQLite was considered as a vector store, but Turbovec would be overkill for this scope.
Our document corpus is too small (in this szenario) to warrant the extra complexity.
[...]
```

```text
[...]
While augments sub-agents work on the seeding and discovery agent scripts, we've been talking back-and-forth with the coordinator agent to clarify subsequent tasks and waves.
Especially in terms of clarifying seeding + embedding -> vector store and retrieval.
[...]
